<pr_description>
$derived reactivity breaks with "createSubscriber" after its teardown/destroy has been called at least once.
### Describe the bug

The reactivity of $derived seems to break in combination with createSubscriber after its teardown has been called once AND if the value it's watching is not being used elsewhere. Using instead a plain (reactive) function seems to work fine, however.   

My apologies if this is intended behavior, and not a bug which it seems to me to be.

     1	import { get, tick, untrack } from '../internal/client/runtime.js';
     2	import { effect_tracking, render_effect } from '../internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
     3	import { source, increment } from '../internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
     4	import { tag } from '../internal/client/dev/tracing.js';
     5	import { DEV } from 'esm-env';
     6	import { queue_micro_task } from '../internal/client/dom/task.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * Returns a `subscribe` function that integrates external event-based systems with Svelte's reactivity.
    10	 * It's particularly useful for integrating with web APIs like `MediaQuery`, `IntersectionObserver`, or `WebSocket`.
    11	 *
    12	 * If `subscribe` is called inside an effect (including indirectly, for example inside a getter),
    13	 * the `start` callback will be called with an `update` function. Whenever `update` is called, the effect re-runs.
    14	 *
    15	 * If `start` returns a cleanup function, it will be called when the effect is destroyed.
    16	 *
    17	 * If `subscribe` is called in multiple effects, `start` will only be called once as long as the effects
    18	 * are active, and the returned teardown function will only be called when all effects are destroyed.
    19	 *
    20	 * It's best understood with an example. Here's an implementation of [`MediaQuery`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-reactivity#MediaQuery):
    21	 *
    22	 * ```js
    23	 * import { createSubscriber } from 'svelte/reactivity';
    24	 * import { on } from 'svelte/events';
    25	 *
    26	 * export class MediaQuery {
    27	 *      #query;
    28	 *      #subscribe;
    29	 *
    30	 *      constructor(query) {
    31	 *              this.#query = window.matchMedia(`(${query})`);
    32	 *
    33	 *              this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
    34	 *                      // when the `change` event occurs, re-run any effects that read `this.current`
    35	 *                      const off = on(this.#query, 'change', update);
    36	 *
    37	 *                      // stop listening when all the effects are destroyed
    38	 *                      return () => off();
    39	 *              });
    40	 *      }
    41	 *
    42	 *      get current() {
    43	 *              // This makes the getter reactive, if read in an effect
    44	 *              this.#subscribe();
    45	 *
    46	 *              // Return the current state of the query, whether or not we're in an effect
    47	 *              return this.#query.matches;
    48	 *      }
    49	 * }
    50	 * ```
    51	 * @param {(update: () => void) => (() => void) | void} start
    52	 * @since 5.7.0
    53	 */
    54	export function createSubscriber(start) {
    55	        let subscribers = 0;
    56	        let version = source(0);
    57	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
    58	        let stop;
    59	
    60	        if (DEV) {
    61	                tag(version, 'createSubscriber version');
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return () => {
    65	                if (effect_tracking()) {
    66	                        get(version);
    67	
    68	                        render_effect(() => {
    69	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    70	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
    71	                                }
    72	
    73	                                subscribers += 1;
    74	
    75	                                return () => {
    76	                                        queue_micro_task(() => {
    77	                                                // Only count down after a microtask, else we would reach 0 before our own render effect reruns,
    78	                                                // but reach 1 again when the tick callback of the prior teardown runs. That would mean we
    79	                                                // re-subcribe unnecessarily and create a memory leak because the old subscription is never cleaned up.
    80	                                                subscribers -= 1;
    81	
    82	                                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    83	                                                        stop?.();
    84	                                                        stop = undefined;
    85	                                                }
    86	                                        });
    87	                                };
    88	                        });
    89	                }
    90	        };
    91	}
    92

    26	 * @template V

    31	/**
    32	 * Create a store from a function that returns state, and (to make a writable store), an
    33	 * optional second function that sets state.
    34	 *
    35	 * ```ts
    36	 * import { toStore } from 'svelte/store';
    37	 *
    38	 * let count = $state(0);
    39	 *
    40	 * const store = toStore(() => count, (v) => (count = v));
    41	 * ```
    42	 * @template V
    43	 * @param {() => V} get
    44	 * @param {(v: V) => void} [set]
    45	 * @returns {Writable<V> | Readable<V>}
    46	 */
    47	export function toStore(get, set) {
    48	        var effect = active_effect;
    49	        var reaction = active_reaction;
    50	        var init_value = get();
    51	
    52	        const store = writable(init_value, (set) => {
    53	                // If the value has changed before we call subscribe, then
    54	                // we need to treat the value as already having run
    55	                var ran = init_value !== get();
    56	
    57	                // TODO do we need a different implementation on the server?
    58	                var teardown;
    59	                // Apply the reaction and effect at the time of toStore being called
    60	                var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
    61	                var previous_effect = active_effect;
    62	                set_active_reaction(reaction);
    63	                set_active_effect(effect);
    64	
    65	                try {
    66	                        teardown = effect_root(() => {
    67	                                render_effect(() => {
    68	                                        const value = get();
    69	                                        if (ran) set(value);
    70	                                });
    71	                        });
    72	                } finally {
    73	                        set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
    74	                        set_active_effect(previous_effect);
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                ran = true;
    78	
    79	                return teardown;
    80	        });
    81	
    82	        if (set) {
    83	                return {
    84	                        set,
    85	                        update: (fn) => set(fn(get())),
    86	                        subscribe: store.subscribe
    87	                };
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        return {
    91	                subscribe: store.subscribe
    92	        };
    93	}
    94	
    95	/**
    96	 * @template V
    97	 * @overload
    98	 * @param {Writable<V>} store
    99	 * @returns {{ current: V }}
   100	 */

   102	 * @template V
   103	 * @overload
   104	 * @param {Readable<V>} store
   105	 * @returns {{ readonly current: V }}
   106	 */
   107	/**
   108	 * Convert a store to an object with a reactive `current` property. If `store`
   109	 * is a readable store, `current` will be a readonly property.
   110	 *
   111	 * ```ts
   112	 * import { fromStore, get, writable } from 'svelte/store';
   113	 *
   114	 * const store = writable(0);
   115	 *
   116	 * const count = fromStore(store);
   117	 *
   118	 * count.current; // 0;
   119	 * store.set(1);
   120	 * count.current; // 1
   121	 *
   122	 * count.current += 1;
   123	 * get(store); // 2
   124	 * ```
   125	 * @template V
   126	 * @param {Writable<V> | Readable<V>} store
   127	 */
   128	export function fromStore(store) {
   129	        let value = /** @type {V} */ (undefined);
   130	
   131	        const subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
   132	                let ran = false;
   133	
   134	                const unsubscribe = store.subscribe((v) => {
   135	                        value = v;
   136	                        if (ran) update();
   137	                });
   138	
   139	                ran = true;
   140	
   141	                return unsubscribe;
   142	        });
   143	
   144	        function current() {
   145	                if (effect_tracking()) {
   146	                        subscribe();
   147	                        return value;
   148	                }
   149	
   150	                return get(store);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if ('set' in store) {
   154	                return {
   155	                        get current() {
   156	                                return current();
   157	                        },
   158	                        set current(v) {
   159	                                store.set(v);
   160	                        }
   161	                };
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        return {
   165	                get current() {
   166	                        return current();
   167	                }
   168	        };
   169	}

import { createSubscriber } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js'"'"';
import { source, set } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js'"'"';
import { effect_root, render_effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { derived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { flushSync } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/index-client.js'"'"';

// Mocking some environment since we are running in node
globalThis.window = globalThis;

async function test() {
    let count = source(0);
    let subscriberCalled = 0;
    let teardownCalled = 0;

    const subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
        subscriberCalled++;
        const interval = setInterval(() => {
            update();
        }, 10);
        return () => {
            teardownCalled++;
            clearInterval(interval);
        };
    });

    const d = effect_root(() => {
        return derived(() => {
            subscribe();
            return count.v;
        });
    });

    // 1. Initial run
    let root = effect_root(() => {
        render_effect(() => {
            d.v;
            // console.log('"'"'derived value:'"'"', d.v);
        });
    });
    
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After 1st run: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);

    // 2. Destroy and teardown
    root();
    flushSync();
    
    // Wait for microtask in createSubscriber
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
    console.log('"'"'After 1st destroy: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);

    // 3. Re-run
    root = effect_root(() => {
        render_effect(() => {
            d.v;
            // console.log('"'"'derived value:'"'"', d.v);
        });
    });
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After 2nd run: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);
    
    // 4. Update count and see if derived updates
    set(count, 1);
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After count update: derived value is'"'"', d.v);
}

test();

    38	        throw_rune_error('$state');
    39	        throw_rune_error('$effect');
    40	        throw_rune_error('$derived');
    41	        throw_rune_error('$inspect');
    42	        throw_rune_error('$props');
    43	        throw_rune_error('$bindable');
    44	}
    45	
    46	/**
    47	 * Returns an [`AbortSignal`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal) that aborts when the current [derived](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$derived) or [effect](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect) re-runs or is destroyed.
    48	 *
    49	 * Must be called while a derived or effect is running.
    50	 *
    51	 * ```svelte
    52	 * <script>
    53	 *      import { getAbortSignal } from 'svelte';
    54	 *
    55	 *      let { id } = $props();
    56	 *
    57	 *      async function getData(id) {
    58	 *              const response = await fetch(`/items/${id}`, {
    59	 *                      signal: getAbortSignal()
    60	 *              });
    61	 *
    62	 *              return await response.json();
    63	 *      }
    64	 *
    65	 *      const data = $derived(await getData(id));
    66	 * </script>
    67	 * ```
    68	 */
    69	export function getAbortSignal() {
    70	        if (active_reaction === null) {
    71	                e.get_abort_signal_outside_reaction();
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        return (active_reaction.ac ??= new AbortController()).signal;
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * `onMount`, like [`$effect`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect), schedules a function to run as soon as the component has been mounted to the DOM.
    79	 * Unlike `$effect`, the provided function only runs once.
    80	 *
    81	 * It must be called during the component's initialisation (but doesn't need to live _inside_ the component;
    82	 * it can be called from an external module). If a function is returned _synchronously_ from `onMount`,
    83	 * it will be called when the component is unmounted.
    84	 *
    85	 * `onMount` functions do not run during [server-side rendering](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-server#render).
    86	 *
    87	 * @template T
    88	 * @param {() => NotFunction<T> | Promise<NotFunction<T>> | (() => any)} fn
    89	 * @returns {void}
    90	 */
    91	export function onMount(fn) {
    92	        if (component_context === null) {
    93	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('onMount');
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        if (legacy_mode_flag && component_context.l !== null) {
    97	                init_update_callbacks(component_context).m.push(fn);
    98	        } else {
    99	                user_effect(() => {
   100	                        const cleanup = untrack(fn);
   101	                        if (typeof cleanup === 'function') return /** @type {() => void} */ (cleanup);
   102	                });
   103	        }
   104	}
   105	
   106	/**
   107	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately before the component is unmounted.
   108	 *
   109	 * Out of `onMount`, `beforeUpdate`, `afterUpdate` and `onDestroy`, this is the
   110	 * only one that runs inside a server-side component.
   111	 *
   112	 * @param {() => any} fn
   113	 * @returns {void}
   114	 */
   115	export function onDestroy(fn) {
   116	        if (component_context === null) {
   117	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('onDestroy');
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        onMount(() => () => untrack(fn));
   121	}
   122	
   123	/**
   124	 * @template [T=any]
   125	 * @param {string} type
   126	 * @param {T} [detail]
   127	 * @param {any}params_0
   128	 * @returns {CustomEvent<T>}
   129	 */
   130	function create_custom_event(type, detail, { bubbles = false, cancelable = false } = {}) {
   131	        return new CustomEvent(type, { detail, bubbles, cancelable });
   132	}
   133	
   134	/**
   135	 * Creates an event dispatcher that can be used to dispatch [component events](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/legacy-on#Component-events).
   136	 * Event dispatchers are functions that can take two arguments: `name` and `detail`.
   137	 *
   138	 * Component events created with `createEventDispatcher` create a
   139	 * [CustomEvent](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent).
   140	 * These events do not [bubble](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/JavaScript/Building_blocks/Events#Event_bubbling_and_capture).
   141	 * The `detail` argument corresponds to the [CustomEvent.detail](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent/detail)
   142	 * property and can contain any type of data.
   143	 *
   144	 * The event dispatcher can be typed to narrow the allowed event names and the type of the `detail` argument:
   145	 * ```ts
   146	 * const dispatch = createEventDispatcher<{
   147	 *  loaded: null; // does not take a detail argument
   148	 *  change: string; // takes a detail argument of type string, which is required
   149	 *  optional: number | null; // takes an optional detail argument of type number
   150	 * }>();
   151	 * ```
   152	 *
   153	 * @deprecated Use callback props and/or the `$host()` rune instead — see [migration guide](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/v5-migration-guide#Event-changes-Component-events)
   154	 * @template {Record<string, any>} [EventMap = any]
   155	 * @returns {EventDispatcher<EventMap>}
   156	 */
   157	export function createEventDispatcher() {
   158	        const active_component_context = component_context;
   159	        if (active_component_context === null) {
   160	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('createEventDispatcher');
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        return (type, detail, options) => {
   164	                const events = /** @type {Record<string, Function | Function[]>} */ (
   165	                        active_component_context.s.$$events
   166	                )?.[/** @type {any} */ (type)];
   167	
   168	                if (events) {
   169	                        const callbacks = is_array(events) ? events.slice() : [events];
   170	                        // TODO are there situations where events could be dispatched
   171	                        // in a server (non-DOM) environment?
   172	                        const event = create_custom_event(/** @type {string} */ (type), detail, options);
   173	                        for (const fn of callbacks) {
   174	                                fn.call(active_component_context.x, event);
   175	                        }
   176	                        return !event.defaultPrevented;
   177	                }
   178	
   179	                return true;
   180	        };
   181	}
   182	
   183	// TODO mark beforeUpdate and afterUpdate as deprecated in Svelte 6
   184	
   185	/**
   186	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately before the component is updated after any state change.
   187	 *
   188	 * The first time the callback runs will be before the initial `onMount`.
   189	 *
   190	 * In runes mode use `$effect.pre` instead.
   191	 *
   192	 * @deprecated Use [`$effect.pre`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect#$effect.pre) instead
   193	 * @param {() => void} fn
   194	 * @returns {void}
   195	 */
   196	export function beforeUpdate(fn) {
   197	        if (component_context === null) {
   198	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('beforeUpdate');
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        if (component_context.l === null) {
   202	                e.lifecycle_legacy_only('beforeUpdate');
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        init_update_callbacks(component_context).b.push(fn);
   206	}
   207	
   208	/**
   209	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately after the component has been updated.
   210	 *
   211	 * The first time the callback runs will be after the initial `onMount`.
   212	 *
   213	 * In runes mode use `$effect` instead.
   214	 *
   215	 * @deprecated Use [`$effect`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect) instead
   216	 * @param {() => void} fn
   217	 * @returns {void}
   218	 */
   219	export function afterUpdate(fn) {
   220	        if (component_context === null) {
   221	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('afterUpdate');
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        if (component_context.l === null) {
   225	                e.lifecycle_legacy_only('afterUpdate');
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        init_update_callbacks(component_context).a.push(fn);
   229	}
   230	
   231	/**
   232	 * Legacy-mode: Init callbacks object for onMount/beforeUpdate/afterUpdate
   233	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   234	 */
   235	function init_update_callbacks(context) {
   236	        var l = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (context).l;
   237	        return (l.u ??= { a: [], b: [], m: [] });
   238	}

    46	/**
    47	 * @param {'$effect' | '$effect.pre' | '$inspect'} rune
    48	 */
    49	export function validate_effect(rune) {
    50	        if (active_effect === null && active_reaction === null) {
    51	                e.effect_orphan(rune);
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & UNOWNED) !== 0 && active_effect === null) {
    55	                e.effect_in_unowned_derived();
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        if (is_destroying_effect) {
    59	                e.effect_in_teardown(rune);
    60	        }
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * @param {Effect} effect
    65	 * @param {Effect} parent_effect
    66	 */
    67	function push_effect(effect, parent_effect) {
    68	        var parent_last = parent_effect.last;
    69	        if (parent_last === null) {
    70	                parent_effect.last = parent_effect.first = effect;
    71	        } else {
    72	                parent_last.next = effect;
    73	                effect.prev = parent_last;
    74	                parent_effect.last = effect;
    75	        }
    76	}
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * @param {number} type
    80	 * @param {null | (() => void | (() => void))} fn
    81	 * @param {boolean} sync
    82	 * @param {boolean} push
    83	 * @returns {Effect}
    84	 */
    85	function create_effect(type, fn, sync, push = true) {
    86	        var parent = active_effect;
    87	
    88	        if (DEV) {
    89	                // Ensure the parent is never an inspect effect
    90	                while (parent !== null && (parent.f & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
    91	                        parent = parent.parent;
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        if (parent !== null && (parent.f & INERT) !== 0) {
    96	                type |= INERT;
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        /** @type {Effect} */
   100	        var effect = {
   101	                ctx: component_context,
   102	                deps: null,
   103	                nodes_start: null,
   104	                nodes_end: null,
   105	                f: type | DIRTY,
   106	                first: null,
   107	                fn,
   108	                last: null,
   109	                next: null,
   110	                parent,
   111	                b: parent && parent.b,
   112	                prev: null,
   113	                teardown: null,
   114	                transitions: null,
   115	                wv: 0,
   116	                ac: null
   117	        };
   118	
   119	        if (DEV) {
   120	                effect.component_function = dev_current_component_function;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        if (sync) {
   124	                try {
   125	                        update_effect(effect);
   126	                        effect.f |= EFFECT_RAN;
   127	                } catch (e) {
   128	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   129	                        throw e;
   130	                }
   131	        } else if (fn !== null) {
   132	                schedule_effect(effect);
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        // if an effect has no dependencies, no DOM and no teardown function,
   136	        // don't bother adding it to the effect tree
   137	        var inert =
   138	                sync &&
   139	                effect.deps === null &&
   140	                effect.first === null &&
   141	                effect.nodes_start === null &&
   142	                effect.teardown === null &&
   143	                (effect.f & EFFECT_PRESERVED) === 0;
   144	
   145	        if (!inert && push) {
   146	                if (parent !== null) {
   147	                        push_effect(effect, parent);
   148	                }
   149	
   150	                // if we're in a derived, add the effect there too
   151	                if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   152	                        var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction);
   153	                        (derived.effects ??= []).push(effect);
   154	                }
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        return effect;
   158	}

   247	/**
   248	 * An effect root whose children can transition out
   249	 * @param {() => void} fn
   250	 * @returns {(options?: { outro?: boolean }) => Promise<void>}
   251	 */
   252	export function component_root(fn) {
   253	        Batch.ensure();
   254	        const effect = create_effect(ROOT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   255	
   256	        return (options = {}) => {
   257	                return new Promise((fulfil) => {

   259	                                pause_effect(effect, () => {
   260	                                        destroy_effect(effect);
   261	                                        fulfil(undefined);
   262	                                });
   263	                        } else {
   264	                                destroy_effect(effect);
   265	                                fulfil(undefined);
   266	                        }
   267	                });
   268	        };
   269	}

   279	/**
   280	 * Internal representation of `$: ..`
   281	 * @param {() => any} deps
   282	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   283	 */
   284	export function legacy_pre_effect(deps, fn) {
   285	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   286	
   287	        /** @type {{ effect: null | Effect, ran: boolean, deps: () => any }} */
   288	        var token = { effect: null, ran: false, deps };
   289	
   290	        context.l.$.push(token);
   291	
   292	        token.effect = render_effect(() => {
   293	                deps();
   294	
   295	                // If this legacy pre effect has already run before the end of the reset, then
   296	                // bail out to emulate the same behavior.
   297	                if (token.ran) return;
   298	
   299	                token.ran = true;
   300	                untrack(fn);
   301	        });
   302	}
   303	
   304	export function legacy_pre_effect_reset() {
   305	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   306	
   307	        render_effect(() => {
   308	                // Run dirty `$:` statements
   309	                for (var token of context.l.$) {
   310	                        token.deps();
   311	
   312	                        var effect = token.effect;
   313	
   314	                        // If the effect is CLEAN, then make it MAYBE_DIRTY. This ensures we traverse through
   315	                        // the effects dependencies and correctly ensure each dependency is up-to-date.
   316	                        if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   317	                                set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   318	                        }
   319	
   320	                        if (is_dirty(effect)) {
   321	                                update_effect(effect);
   322	                        }
   323	
   324	                        token.ran = false;
   325	                }
   326	        });
   327	}

   341	export function render_effect(fn, flags = 0) {

   344	
   345	/**
   346	 * @param {(...expressions: any) => void | (() => void)} fn
   347	 * @param {Array<() => any>} sync
   348	 * @param {Array<() => Promise<any>>} async
   349	 */
   350	export function template_effect(fn, sync = [], async = []) {
   351	        flatten(sync, async, (values) => {
   352	                create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT, () => fn(...values.map(get)), true);
   353	        });
   354	}
   355	
   356	/**
   357	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   358	 * @param {number} flags
   359	 */
   360	export function block(fn, flags = 0) {
   361	        var effect = create_effect(BLOCK_EFFECT | flags, fn, true);
   362	        if (DEV) {
   363	                effect.dev_stack = dev_stack;
   364	        }
   365	        return effect;
   366	}
   367	
   368	/**
   369	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   370	 * @param {boolean} [push]
   371	 */
   372	export function branch(fn, push = true) {
   373	        return create_effect(BRANCH_EFFECT, fn, true, push);
   374	}
   375	
   376	/**
   377	 * @param {Effect} effect
   378	 */
   379	export function execute_effect_teardown(effect) {
   380	        var teardown = effect.teardown;
   381	        if (teardown !== null) {
   382	                const previously_destroying_effect = is_destroying_effect;
   383	                const previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   384	                set_is_destroying_effect(true);
   385	                set_active_reaction(null);
   386	                try {
   387	                        teardown.call(null);
   388	                } finally {
   389	                        set_is_destroying_effect(previously_destroying_effect);
   390	                        set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   391	                }
   392	        }
   393	}
   394	
   395	/**
   396	 * @param {Effect} signal
   397	 * @param {boolean} remove_dom
   398	 * @returns {void}
   399	 */
   400	export function destroy_effect_children(signal, remove_dom = false) {
   401	        var effect = signal.first;
   402	        signal.first = signal.last = null;
   403	
   404	        while (effect !== null) {
   405	                effect.ac?.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   406	
   407	                var next = effect.next;
   408	
   409	                if ((effect.f & ROOT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   410	                        // this is now an independent root
   411	                        effect.parent = null;
   412	                } else {
   413	                        destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom);
   414	                }
   415	
   416	                effect = next;
   417	        }
   418	}
   419	
   420	/**
   421	 * @param {Effect} signal
   422	 * @returns {void}
   423	 */
   424	export function destroy_block_effect_children(signal) {
   425	        var effect = signal.first;
   426	
   427	        while (effect !== null) {
   428	                var next = effect.next;
   429	                if ((effect.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) === 0) {
   430	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   431	                }
   432	                effect = next;
   433	        }
   434	}
   435	
   436	/**
   437	 * @param {Effect} effect
   438	 * @param {boolean} [remove_dom]
   439	 * @returns {void}
   440	 */
   441	export function destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom = true) {
   442	        var removed = false;
   443	
   444	        if (
   445	                (remove_dom || (effect.f & HEAD_EFFECT) !== 0) &&
   446	                effect.nodes_start !== null &&
   447	                effect.nodes_end !== null
   448	        ) {
   449	                remove_effect_dom(effect.nodes_start, /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (effect.nodes_end));
   450	                removed = true;
   451	        }
   452	
   453	        destroy_effect_children(effect, remove_dom && !removed);
   454	        remove_reactions(effect, 0);
   455	        set_signal_status(effect, DESTROYED);
   456	
   457	        var transitions = effect.transitions;
   458	
   459	        if (transitions !== null) {
   460	                for (const transition of transitions) {
   461	                        transition.stop();
   462	                }
   463	        }
   464	
   465	        execute_effect_teardown(effect);
   466	
   467	        var parent = effect.parent;
   468	
   469	        // If the parent doesn't have any children, then skip this work altogether
   470	        if (parent !== null && parent.first !== null) {
   471	                unlink_effect(effect);
   472	        }
   473	
   474	        if (DEV) {
   475	                effect.component_function = null;
   476	        }
   477	
   478	        // `first` and `child` are nulled out in destroy_effect_children
   479	        // we don't null out `parent` so that error propagation can work correctly
   480	        effect.next =
   481	                effect.prev =
   482	                effect.teardown =
   483	                effect.ctx =
   484	                effect.deps =
   485	                effect.fn =
   486	                effect.nodes_start =
   487	                effect.nodes_end =
   488	                effect.ac =
   489	                        null;
   490	}
   491	
   492	/**
   493	 *
   494	 * @param {TemplateNode | null} node
   495	 * @param {TemplateNode} end
   496	 */
   497	export function remove_effect_dom(node, end) {
   498	        while (node !== null) {
   499	                /** @type {TemplateNode | null} */
   500	                var next = node === end ? null : /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (get_next_sibling(node));
   501	
   502	                node.remove();
   503	                node = next;
   504	        }
   505	}
   506	
   507	/**
   508	 * Detach an effect from the effect tree, freeing up memory and
   509	 * reducing the amount of work that happens on subsequent traversals
   510	 * @param {Effect} effect
   511	 */
   512	export function unlink_effect(effect) {
   513	        var parent = effect.parent;
   514	        var prev = effect.prev;
   515	        var next = effect.next;
   516	
   517	        if (prev !== null) prev.next = next;
   518	        if (next !== null) next.prev = prev;
   519	
   520	        if (parent !== null) {
   521	                if (parent.first === effect) parent.first = next;
   522	                if (parent.last === effect) parent.last = prev;
   523	        }
   524	}
   525	
   526	/**
   527	 * When a block effect is removed, we don't immediately destroy it or yank it
   528	 * out of the DOM, because it might have transitions. Instead, we 'pause' it.
   529	 * It stays around (in memory, and in the DOM) until outro transitions have
   530	 * completed, and if the state change is reversed then we _resume_ it.
   531	 * A paused effect does not update, and the DOM subtree becomes inert.
   532	 * @param {Effect} effect
   533	 * @param {() => void} [callback]
   534	 */
   535	export function pause_effect(effect, callback) {
   536	        /** @type {TransitionManager[]} */
   537	        var transitions = [];
   538	
   539	        pause_children(effect, transitions, true);
   540	
   541	        run_out_transitions(transitions, () => {
   542	                destroy_effect(effect);
   543	                if (callback) callback();
   544	        });
   545	}
   546	
   547	/**
   548	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   549	 * @param {() => void} fn
   550	 */
   551	export function run_out_transitions(transitions, fn) {
   552	        var remaining = transitions.length;
   553	        if (remaining > 0) {
   554	                var check = () => --remaining || fn();
   555	                for (var transition of transitions) {
   556	                        transition.out(check);
   557	                }
   558	        } else {
   559	                fn();
   560	        }
   561	}
   562	
   563	/**
   564	 * @param {Effect} effect
   565	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   566	 * @param {boolean} local
   567	 */
   568	export function pause_children(effect, transitions, local) {
   569	        if ((effect.f & INERT) !== 0) return;
   570	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   571	
   572	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   573	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   574	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   575	                                transitions.push(transition);
   576	                        }
   577	                }
   578	        }
   579	
   580	        var child = effect.first;
   581	
   582	        while (child !== null) {
   583	                var sibling = child.next;
   584	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   585	                // TODO we don't need to call pause_children recursively with a linked list in place
   586	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   587	                // through the tree.
   588	                pause_children(child, transitions, transparent ? local : false);
   589	                child = sibling;
   590	        }
   591	}
   592	
   593	/**
   594	 * The opposite of `pause_effect`. We call this if (for example)
   595	 * `x` becomes falsy then truthy: `{#if x}...{/if}`
   596	 * @param {Effect} effect
   597	 */
   598	export function resume_effect(effect) {
   599	        resume_children(effect, true);
   600	}
   601	
   602	/**
   603	 * @param {Effect} effect
   604	 * @param {boolean} local
   605	 */
   606	function resume_children(effect, local) {
   607	        if ((effect.f & INERT) === 0) return;
   608	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   609	
   610	        // If a dependency of this effect changed while it was paused,
   611	        // schedule the effect to update. we don't use `is_dirty`
   612	        // here because we don't want to eagerly recompute a derived like
   613	        // `{#if foo}{foo.bar()}{/if}` if `foo` is now `undefined
   614	        if ((effect.f & CLEAN) === 0) {
   615	                set_signal_status(effect, DIRTY);
   616	                schedule_effect(effect);
   617	        }
   618	
   619	        var child = effect.first;
   620	
   621	        while (child !== null) {
   622	                var sibling = child.next;
   623	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   624	                // TODO we don't need to call resume_children recursively with a linked list in place
   625	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   626	                // through the tree.
   627	                resume_children(child, transparent ? local : false);
   628	                child = sibling;
   629	        }
   630	
   631	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   632	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   633	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   634	                                transition.in();
   635	                        }
   636	                }
   637	        }
   638	}
   639	
   640	export function aborted() {
   641	        var effect = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
   642	        return (effect.f & DESTROYED) !== 0;
   643	}
   644

   276	        var parent = derived.parent;
   277	        while (parent !== null) {
   278	                if ((parent.f & DERIVED) === 0) {
   279	                        return /** @type {Effect} */ (parent);
   280	                }
   281	                parent = parent.parent;

   291	export function execute_derived(derived) {
   292	        var value;
   293	        var prev_active_effect = active_effect;
   294	
   295	        set_active_effect(get_derived_parent_effect(derived));
   296

   298	                let prev_inspect_effects = inspect_effects;

   301	                        if (stack.includes(derived)) {
   302	                                e.derived_references_self();
   303	                        }
   304	
   305	                        stack.push(derived);
   306	
   307	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   308	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   309	                } finally {
   310	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   311	                        set_inspect_effects(prev_inspect_effects);
   312	                        stack.pop();
   313	                }
   314	        } else {
   315	                try {
   316	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   317	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   318	                } finally {
   319	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   320	                }
   321	        }
   322	
   323	        return value;
   324	}

   329	 */
   330	export function update_derived(derived) {
   331	        var value = execute_derived(derived);
   332	
   333	        if (!derived.equals(value)) {
   334	                derived.v = value;
   335	                derived.wv = increment_write_version();

   338	        // don't mark derived clean if we're reading it inside a
   339	        // cleanup function, or it will cache a stale value

   341	                return;

    93	                        current_sources = [value];
    94	                } else {
    95	                        current_sources.push(value);
    96	                }
    97	        }
    98	}
    99	
   100	/**
   101	 * The dependencies of the reaction that is currently being executed. In many cases,
   102	 * the dependencies are unchanged between runs, and so this will be `null` unless
   103	 * and until a new dependency is accessed — we track this via `skipped_deps`
   104	 * @type {null | Value[]}
   105	 */
   106	let new_deps = null;
   107	
   108	let skipped_deps = 0;
   109	
   110	/**
   111	 * Tracks writes that the effect it's executed in doesn't listen to yet,
   112	 * so that the dependency can be added to the effect later on if it then reads it
   113	 * @type {null | Source[]}
   114	 */
   115	export let untracked_writes = null;
   116	
   117	/** @param {null | Source[]} value */
   118	export function set_untracked_writes(value) {
   119	        untracked_writes = value;
   120	}
   121	
   122	/**
   123	 * @type {number} Used by sources and deriveds for handling updates.
   124	 * Version starts from 1 so that unowned deriveds differentiate between a created effect and a run one for tracing
   125	 **/
   126	export let write_version = 1;
   127	
   128	/** @type {number} Used to version each read of a source of derived to avoid duplicating depedencies inside a reaction */
   129	let read_version = 0;
   130	
   131	export let update_version = read_version;
   132	
   133	/** @param {number} value */
   134	export function set_update_version(value) {
   135	        update_version = value;
   136	}
   137	
   138	// If we are working with a get() chain that has no active container,
   139	// to prevent memory leaks, we skip adding the reaction.
   140	export let skip_reaction = false;
   141	
   142	export function increment_write_version() {
   143	        return ++write_version;
   144	}
   145	
   146	/**
   147	 * Determines whether a derived or effect is dirty.
   148	 * If it is MAYBE_DIRTY, will set the status to CLEAN
   149	 * @param {Reaction} reaction
   150	 * @returns {boolean}
   151	 */
   152	export function is_dirty(reaction) {
   153	        var flags = reaction.f;
   154	
   155	        if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   156	                return true;
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if ((flags & MAYBE_DIRTY) !== 0) {
   160	                var dependencies = reaction.deps;
   161	                var is_unowned = (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0;
   162	
   163	                if (dependencies !== null) {
   164	                        var i;
   165	                        var dependency;
   166	                        var is_disconnected = (flags & DISCONNECTED) !== 0;
   167	                        var is_unowned_connected = is_unowned && active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction;
   168	                        var length = dependencies.length;
   169	
   170	                        // If we are working with a disconnected or an unowned signal that is now connected (due to an active effect)
   171	                        // then we need to re-connect the reaction to the dependency, unless the effect has already been destroyed
   172	                        // (which can happen if the derived is read by an async derived)
   173	                        if (
   174	                                (is_disconnected || is_unowned_connected) &&
   175	                                (active_effect === null || (active_effect.f & DESTROYED) === 0)
   176	                        ) {
   177	                                var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (reaction);
   178	                                var parent = derived.parent;
   179	
   180	                                for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   181	                                        dependency = dependencies[i];
   182	
   183	                                        // We always re-add all reactions (even duplicates) if the derived was
   184	                                        // previously disconnected, however we don't if it was unowned as we
   185	                                        // de-duplicate dependencies in that case
   186	                                        if (is_disconnected || !dependency?.reactions?.includes(derived)) {
   187	                                                (dependency.reactions ??= []).push(derived);
   188	                                        }
   189	                                }
   190	
   191	                                if (is_disconnected) {
   192	                                        derived.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   193	                                }
   194	                                // If the unowned derived is now fully connected to the graph again (it's unowned and reconnected, has a parent
   195	                                // and the parent is not unowned), then we can mark it as connected again, removing the need for the unowned
   196	                                // flag
   197	                                if (is_unowned_connected && parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
   198	                                        derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
   199	                                }
   200	                        }
   201	
   202	                        for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   203	                                dependency = dependencies[i];
   204	
   205	                                if (is_dirty(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency))) {
   206	                                        update_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency));
   207	                                }
   208	
   209	                                if (dependency.wv > reaction.wv) {
   210	                                        return true;
   211	                                }
   212	                        }
   213	                }
   214	
   215	                // Unowned signals should never be marked as clean unless they
   216	                // are used within an active_effect without skip_reaction
   217	                if (!is_unowned || (active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction)) {
   218	                        set_signal_status(reaction, CLEAN);
   219	                }
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        return false;
   223	}
   224	
   225	/**
   226	 * @param {Value} signal
   227	 * @param {Effect} effect
   228	 * @param {boolean} [root]
   229	 */
   230	function schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(signal, effect, root = true) {
   231	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   232	        if (reactions === null) return;
   233	
   234	        if (!async_mode_flag && current_sources?.includes(signal)) {
   235	                return;
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        for (var i = 0; i < reactions.length; i++) {
   239	                var reaction = reactions[i];
   240	
   241	                if ((reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   242	                        schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), effect, false);
   243	                } else if (effect === reaction) {
   244	                        if (root) {
   245	                                set_signal_status(reaction, DIRTY);
   246	                        } else if ((reaction.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   247	                                set_signal_status(reaction, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   248	                        }
   249	                        schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   250	                }
   251	        }
   252	}
   253	
   254	/** @param {Reaction} reaction */
   255	export function update_reaction(reaction) {
   256	        var previous_deps = new_deps;
   257	        var previous_skipped_deps = skipped_deps;
   258	        var previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   259	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   260	        var previous_skip_reaction = skip_reaction;
   261	        var previous_sources = current_sources;
   262	        var previous_component_context = component_context;
   263	        var previous_untracking = untracking;
   264	        var previous_update_version = update_version;
   265	
   266	        var flags = reaction.f;
   267	
   268	        new_deps = /** @type {null | Value[]} */ (null);
   269	        skipped_deps = 0;
   270	        untracked_writes = null;
   271	        skip_reaction =
   272	                (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0 && (untracking || !is_updating_effect || active_reaction === null);
   273	        active_reaction = (flags & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0 ? reaction : null;
   274	
   275	        current_sources = null;
   276	        set_component_context(reaction.ctx);
   277	        untracking = false;
   278	        update_version = ++read_version;
   279	
   280	        if (reaction.ac !== null) {
   281	                reaction.ac.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   282	                reaction.ac = null;
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        try {
   286	                reaction.f |= REACTION_IS_UPDATING;
   287	                var result = /** @type {Function} */ (0, reaction.fn)();
   288	                var deps = reaction.deps;
   289	
   290	                if (new_deps !== null) {
   291	                        var i;
   292	
   293	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   294	
   295	                        if (deps !== null && skipped_deps > 0) {
   296	                                deps.length = skipped_deps + new_deps.length;
   297	                                for (i = 0; i < new_deps.length; i++) {
   298	                                        deps[skipped_deps + i] = new_deps[i];
   299	                                }
   300	                        } else {
   301	                                reaction.deps = deps = new_deps;
   302	                        }
   303	
   304	                        if (
   305	                                !skip_reaction ||
   306	                                // Deriveds that already have reactions can cleanup, so we still add them as reactions
   307	                                ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   308	                                        /** @type {import('#client').Derived} */ (reaction).reactions !== null)
   309	                        ) {
   310	                                for (i = skipped_deps; i < deps.length; i++) {
   311	                                        (deps[i].reactions ??= []).push(reaction);
   312	                                }
   313	                        }
   314	                } else if (deps !== null && skipped_deps < deps.length) {
   315	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   316	                        deps.length = skipped_deps;
   317	                }
   318	
   319	                // If we're inside an effect and we have untracked writes, then we need to
   320	                // ensure that if any of those untracked writes result in re-invalidation
   321	                // of the current effect, then that happens accordingly
   322	                if (
   323	                        is_runes() &&
   324	                        untracked_writes !== null &&
   325	                        !untracking &&
   326	                        deps !== null &&
   327	                        (reaction.f & (DERIVED | MAYBE_DIRTY | DIRTY)) === 0
   328	                ) {
   329	                        for (i = 0; i < /** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes).length; i++) {
   330	                                schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(
   331	                                        untracked_writes[i],
   332	                                        /** @type {Effect} */ (reaction)
   333	                                );
   334	                        }
   335	                }
   336	
   337	                // If we are returning to an previous reaction then
   338	                // we need to increment the read version to ensure that
   339	                // any dependencies in this reaction aren't marked with
   340	                // the same version
   341	                if (previous_reaction !== null && previous_reaction !== reaction) {
   342	                        read_version++;
   343	
   344	                        if (untracked_writes !== null) {
   345	                                if (previous_untracked_writes === null) {
   346	                                        previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   347	                                } else {
   348	                                        previous_untracked_writes.push(.../** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes));
   349	                                }
   350	                        }
   351	                }
   352	
   353	                if ((reaction.f & ERROR_VALUE) !== 0) {
   354	                        reaction.f ^= ERROR_VALUE;
   355	                }
   356	
   357	                return result;
   358	        } catch (error) {
   359	                return handle_error(error);
   360	        } finally {
   361	                reaction.f ^= REACTION_IS_UPDATING;
   362	                new_deps = previous_deps;
   363	                skipped_deps = previous_skipped_deps;
   364	                untracked_writes = previous_untracked_writes;
   365	                active_reaction = previous_reaction;
   366	                skip_reaction = previous_skip_reaction;
   367	                current_sources = previous_sources;
   368	                set_component_context(previous_component_context);
   369	                untracking = previous_untracking;
   370	                update_version = previous_update_version;
   371	        }
   372	}
   373	
   374	/**
   375	 * @template V
   376	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   377	 * @param {Value<V>} dependency
   378	 * @returns {void}
   379	 */
   380	function remove_reaction(signal, dependency) {
   381	        let reactions = dependency.reactions;
   382	        if (reactions !== null) {
   383	                var index = index_of.call(reactions, signal);
   384	                if (index !== -1) {
   385	                        var new_length = reactions.length - 1;
   386	                        if (new_length === 0) {
   387	                                reactions = dependency.reactions = null;
   388	                        } else {
   389	                                // Swap with last element and then remove.
   390	                                reactions[index] = reactions[new_length];
   391	                                reactions.pop();
   392	                        }
   393	                }
   394	        }
   395	
   396	        // If the derived has no reactions, then we can disconnect it from the graph,
   397	        // allowing it to either reconnect in the future, or be GC'd by the VM.
   398	        if (
   399	                reactions === null &&
   400	                (dependency.f & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   401	                // Destroying a child effect while updating a parent effect can cause a dependency to appear
   402	                // to be unused, when in fact it is used by the currently-updating parent. Checking `new_deps`
   403	                // allows us to skip the expensive work of disconnecting and immediately reconnecting it
   404	                (new_deps === null || !new_deps.includes(dependency))
   405	        ) {
   406	                set_signal_status(dependency, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   407	                // If we are working with a derived that is owned by an effect, then mark it as being
   408	                // disconnected.
   409	                if ((dependency.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {
   410	                        dependency.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   411	                }
   412	                // Disconnect any reactions owned by this reaction
   413	                destroy_derived_effects(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency));
   414	                remove_reactions(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency), 0);
   415	        }
   416	}
   417	
   418	/**
   419	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   420	 * @param {number} start_index
   421	 * @returns {void}
   422	 */
   423	export function remove_reactions(signal, start_index) {
   424	        var dependencies = signal.deps;
   425	        if (dependencies === null) return;
   426	
   427	        for (var i = start_index; i < dependencies.length; i++) {
   428	                remove_reaction(signal, dependencies[i]);
   429	        }
   430	}
   431	
   432	/**
   433	 * @param {Effect} effect
   434	 * @returns {void}
   435	 */
   436	export function update_effect(effect) {
   437	        var flags = effect.f;
   438	
   439	        if ((flags & DESTROYED) !== 0) {
   440	                return;
   441	        }
   442	
   443	        set_signal_status(effect, CLEAN);
   444	
   445	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   446	        var was_updating_effect = is_updating_effect;
   447	
   448	        active_effect = effect;
   449	        is_updating_effect = true;
   450	
   451	        if (DEV) {
   452	                var previous_component_fn = dev_current_component_function;
   453	                set_dev_current_component_function(effect.component_function);
   454	                var previous_stack = /** @type {any} */ (dev_stack);
   455	                // only block effects have a dev stack, keep the current one otherwise
   456	                set_dev_stack(effect.dev_stack ?? dev_stack);
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        try {
   460	                if ((flags & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   461	                        destroy_block_effect_children(effect);
   462	                } else {
   463	                        destroy_effect_children(effect);
   464	                }
   465	
   466	                execute_effect_teardown(effect);
   467	                var teardown = update_reaction(effect);
   468	                effect.teardown = typeof teardown === 'function' ? teardown : null;
   469	                effect.wv = write_version;
   470	
   471	                // In DEV, increment versions of any sources that were written to during the effect,
   472	                // so that they are correctly marked as dirty when the effect re-runs
   473	                if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag && (effect.f & DIRTY) !== 0 && effect.deps !== null) {
   474	                        for (var dep of effect.deps) {
   475	                                if (dep.set_during_effect) {
   476	                                        dep.wv = increment_write_version();
   477	                                        dep.set_during_effect = false;
   478	                                }
   479	                        }
   480	                }
   481	        } finally {
   482	                is_updating_effect = was_updating_effect;
   483	                active_effect = previous_effect;
   484	
   485	                if (DEV) {
   486	                        set_dev_current_component_function(previous_component_fn);
   487	                        set_dev_stack(previous_stack);
   488	                }
   489	        }
   490	}
   491	
   492	/**
   493	 * Returns a promise that resolves once any pending state changes have been applied.
   494	 * @returns {Promise<void>}
   495	 */
   496	export async function tick() {
   497	        if (async_mode_flag) {
   498	                return new Promise((f) => requestAnimationFrame(() => f()));
   499	        }
   500	
   501	        await Promise.resolve();
   502	
   503	        // By calling flushSync we guarantee that any pending state changes are applied after one tick.
   504	        // TODO look into whether we can make flushing subsequent updates synchronously in the future.
   505	        flushSync();
   506	}
   507	
   508	/**
   509	 * Returns a promise that resolves once any state changes, and asynchronous work resulting from them,
   510	 * have resolved and the DOM has been updated
   511	 * @returns {Promise<void>}
   512	 * @since 5.36
   513	 */
   514	export function settled() {
   515	        return Batch.ensure().settled();
   516	}
   517	
   518	/**
   519	 * @template V
   520	 * @param {Value<V>} signal
   521	 * @returns {V}
   522	 */
   523	export function get(signal) {
   524	        var flags = signal.f;
   525	        var is_derived = (flags & DERIVED) !== 0;
   526	
   527	        captured_signals?.add(signal);
   528	
   529	        // Register the dependency on the current reaction signal.
   530	        if (active_reaction !== null && !untracking) {
   531	                // if we're in a derived that is being read inside an _async_ derived,
   532	                // it's possible that the effect was already destroyed. In this case,
   533	                // we don't add the dependency, because that would create a memory leak
   534	                var destroyed = active_effect !== null && (active_effect.f & DESTROYED) !== 0;
   535	
   536	                if (!destroyed && !current_sources?.includes(signal)) {
   537	                        var deps = active_reaction.deps;
   538	
   539	                        if ((active_reaction.f & REACTION_IS_UPDATING) !== 0) {
   540	                                // we're in the effect init/update cycle
   541	                                if (signal.rv < read_version) {
   542	                                        signal.rv = read_version;

   545	                                        // order as it did last time, incre<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. import { createSubscriber } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js'"'"';
import { source, set } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js'"'"';
import { effect_root, render_effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { derived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { flushSync } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/index-client.js'"'"';

// Mocking some environment since we are running in node
globalThis.window = globalThis;

async function test() {
    let count = source(0);
    let subscriberCalled = 0;
    let teardownCalled = 0;

    const subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
        subscriberCalled++;
        const interval = setInterval(() => {
            update();
        }, 10);
        return () => {
            teardownCalled++;
            clearInterval(interval);
        };
    });

    const d = derived(() => {
        subscribe();
        return count.v;
    });

    // 1. Initial run
    let root = effect_root(() => {
        render_effect(() => {
            d.v;
            // console.log('"'"'derived value:'"'"', d.v);
        });
    });
    
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After 1st run: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);

    // 2. Destroy and teardown
    root();
    flushSync();
    
    // Wait for microtask in createSubscriber
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
    console.log('"'"'After 1st destroy: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);

    // 3. Re-run
    root = effect_root(() => {
        render_effect(() => {
            d.v;
            // console.log('"'"'derived value:'"'"', d.v);
        });
    });
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After 2nd run: subscriberCalled'"'"', subscriberCalled, '"'"'teardownCalled'"'"', teardownCalled);
    
    // 4. Update count and see if derived updates
    set(count, 1);
    flushSync();
    console.log('"'"'After count update: derived value is'"'"', d.v);
}

async function test() {
    let count = source(0);
    let subscriberCalled = 0;

	export function createSubscriber(start) {
	        let subscribers = 0;
	        let version = source(0);
	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
	        let stop;
	
	        if (DEV) {
	                tag(version, '"'"'createSubscriber version'"'"');
	        }
	
	        return () => {
	                if (effect_tracking()) {
	                        get(version);
	
	                        render_effect(() => {
	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
	                                }
	
	                                subscribers += 1;
	
	                                return () => {
	                                        queue_micro_task(() => {
	                                                // Only count down after a microtask, else we would reach 0 before our own render effect reruns,
	                                                // but reach 1 again when the tick callback of the prior teardown runs. That would mean we
	                                                // re-subcribe unnecessarily and create a memory leak because the old subscription is never cleaned up.
	                                                subscribers -= 1;
	
	                                                if (subscribers === 0) {
	                                                        stop?.();
	                                                        stop = undefined;
	                                                }
	                                        });
	                                };
	                        });

	                tag(version, '"'"'createSubscriber version'"'"');
	        }

	                if (effect_tracking()) {
	                        get(version);
	
	                        render_effect(() => {
	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => {

	export function createSubscriber(start) {
	        let subscribers = 0;
	        let version = source(0);
	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
	        let stop;
	
	        if (DEV) {
	                tag(version, '"'"'createSubscriber version'"'"');
	        }
	
	        return () => {
	                if (effect_tracking()) {
	                        get(version);
	
	                        render_effect(() => {
	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
	                                }
	
	                                subscribers += 1;
	
	                                return () => {

	                                                        stop?.();
	                                                        stop = undefined;
	                                                }
	                                        });
	                                };
	                        });
	                }

     2	import { effect_tracking, render_effect } from '../internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
     3	import { source, increment } from '../internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
     4	import { tag } from '../internal/client/dev/tracing.js';
     5	import { DEV } from 'esm-env';
     6	import { queue_micro_task } from '../internal/client/dom/task.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * Returns a `subscribe` function that integrates external event-based systems with Svelte's reactivity.
    10	 * It's particularly useful for integrating with web APIs like `MediaQuery`, `IntersectionObserver`, or `WebSocket`.
    11	 *
    12	 * If `subscribe` is called inside an effect (including indirectly, for example inside a getter),
    13	 * the `start` callback will be called with an `update` function. Whenever `update` is called, the effect re-runs.
    14	 *
    15	 * If `start` returns a cleanup function, it will be called when the effect is destroyed.
    16	 *
    17	 * If `subscribe` is called in multiple effects, `start` will only be called once as long as the effects
    18	 * are active, and the returned teardown function will only be called when all effects are destroyed.
    19	 *
    20	 * It's best understood with an example. Here's an implementation of [`MediaQuery`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-reactivity#MediaQuery):
    21	 *
    22	 * ```js
    23	 * import { createSubscriber } from 'svelte/reactivity';
    24	 * import { on } from 'svelte/events';
    25	 *
    26	 * export class MediaQuery {
    27	 *      #query;
    28	 *      #subscribe;
    29	 *
    30	 *      constructor(query) {
    31	 *              this.#query = window.matchMedia(`(${query})`);
    32	 *
    33	 *              this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
    34	 *                      // when the `change` event occurs, re-run any effects that read `this.current`
    35	 *                      const off = on(this.#query, 'change', update);
    36	 *
    37	 *                      // stop listening when all the effects are destroyed
    38	 *                      return () => off();
    39	 *              });
    40	 *      }
    41	 *
    42	 *      get current() {
    43	 *              // This makes the getter reactive, if read in an effect
    44	 *              this.#subscribe();
    45	 *
    46	 *              // Return the current state of the query, whether or not we're in an effect
    47	 *              return this.#query.matches;
    48	 *      }
    49	 * }
    50	 * ```
    51	 * @param {(update: () => void) => (() => void) | void} start
    52	 * @since 5.7.0
    53	 */
    54	export function createSubscriber(start) {
    55	        let subscribers = 0;
    56	        let version = source(0);
    57	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
    58	        let stop;
    59	
    60	        if (DEV) {
    61	                tag(version, 'createSubscriber version');
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return () => {
    65	                if (effect_tracking()) {
    66	                        get(version);
    67	
    68	                        render_effect(() => {
    69	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    70	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
    71	                                }
    72	
    73	                                subscribers += 1;
    74	
    75	                                return () => {
    76	                                        subscribers -= 1;
    77	
    78	                                        if (subscribers === 0) {
    79	                                                queue_micro_task(() => {
    80	                                                        if (subscribers === 0) {
    81	                                                                stop?.();
    82	                                                                stop = undefined;
    83	                                                        }
    84	                                                });
    85	                                        }
    86	                                };
    87	                        });
    88	                }
    89	        };
    90	}

	let subscribers = 0;
	let version = source(0);
	/** @type {(() => void) | void} */
	let stop;

	if (DEV) {
		tag(version, '"'"'createSubscriber version'"'"');
	}

	return () => {
		if (effect_tracking()) {
			get(version);

			render_effect(() => {
				if (subscribers === 0) {
					stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
				}

				subscribers += 1;

				return () => {
					queue_micro_task(() => {
						// Only count down after a microtask, else we would reach 0 before our own render effect reruns,
						// but reach 1 again when the tick callback of the prior teardown runs. That would mean we
						// re-subcribe unnecessarily and create a memory leak because the old subscription is never cleaned up.
						subscribers -= 1;

						if (subscribers === 0) {
							stop?.();
							stop = undefined;
						}
					});
				};
			});
		}
	};

No replacement was performed, old_str `export function createSubscriber(start) {
let subscribers = 0;
let version = source(0);
/** @type {(() => void) | void} */
let stop;

if (DEV) {
tag(version, 'createSubscriber version');
}

return () => {
if (effect_tracking()) {
get(version);

render_effect(() => {
if (subscribers === 0) {
stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
}

subscribers += 1;

return () => {
queue_micro_task(() => {
// Only count down after a microtask, else we would reach 0 before our own render effect reruns,
// but reach 1 again when the tick callback of the prior teardown runs. That would mean we
// re-subcribe unnecessarily and create a memory leak because the old subscription is never cleaned up.
subscribers -= 1;

if (subscribers === 0) {
stop?.();
stop = undefined;
}
});
};
});
}
};
}` did not appear verbatim in /testbed/packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js.

     2	import { effect_tracking, render_effect } from '../internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
     3	import { source, increment } from '../internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
     4	import { tag } from '../internal/client/dev/tracing.js';
     5	import { DEV } from 'esm-env';
     6	import { queue_micro_task } from '../internal/client/dom/task.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * Returns a `subscribe` function that integrates external event-based systems with Svelte's reactivity.
    10	 * It's particularly useful for integrating with web APIs like `MediaQuery`, `IntersectionObserver`, or `WebSocket`.
    11	 *
    12	 * If `subscribe` is called inside an effect (including indirectly, for example inside a getter),
    13	 * the `start` callback will be called with an `update` function. Whenever `update` is called, the effect re-runs.
    14	 *
    15	 * If `start` returns a cleanup function, it will be called when the effect is destroyed.
    16	 *
    17	 * If `subscribe` is called in multiple effects, `start` will only be called once as long as the effects
    18	 * are active, and the returned teardown function will only be called when all effects are destroyed.
    19	 *
    20	 * It's best understood with an example. Here's an implementation of [`MediaQuery`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-reactivity#MediaQuery):
    21	 *
    22	 * ```js
    23	 * import { createSubscriber } from 'svelte/reactivity';
    24	 * import { on } from 'svelte/events';
    25	 *
    26	 * export class MediaQuery {
    27	 *      #query;
    28	 *      #subscribe;
    29	 *
    30	 *      constructor(query) {
    31	 *              this.#query = window.matchMedia(`(${query})`);
    32	 *
    33	 *              this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
    34	 *                      // when the `change` event occurs, re-run any effects that read `this.current`
    35	 *                      const off = on(this.#query, 'change', update);
    36	 *
    37	 *                      // stop listening when all the effects are destroyed
    38	 *                      return () => off();
    39	 *              });
    40	 *      }
    41	 *
    42	 *      get current() {
    43	 *              // This makes the getter reactive, if read in an effect
    44	 *              this.#subscribe();
    45	 *
    46	 *              // Return the current state of the query, whether or not we're in an effect
    47	 *              return this.#query.matches;
    48	 *      }
    49	 * }
    50	 * ```
    51	 * @param {(update: () => void) => (() => void) | void} start
    52	 * @since 5.7.0
    53	 */
    54	export function createSubscriber(start) {
    55	        let subscribers = 0;
    56	        let version = source(0);
    57	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
    58	        let stop;
    59	
    60	        if (DEV) {
    61	                tag(version, 'createSubscriber version');
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return () => {
    65	                if (effect_tracking()) {
    66	                        get(version);
    67	
    68	                        render_effect(() => {
    69	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    70	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
    71	                                }
    72	
    73	                                subscribers += 1;
    74	
    75	                                return () => {
    76	                                        subscribers -= 1;
    77

    80	                                                        if (subscribers === 0) {

    82	                                                                stop = undefined;
